# Task: Implement PolicyQuotaController for Cilium

## Objective
Create a `PolicyQuotaController` in Cilium that enforces per-namespace limits on the
number of `CiliumNetworkPolicy` resources, preventing policy sprawl in multi-tenant clusters.

## Requirements

1. **Create `pkg/policy/quota/controller.go`** with:
   - `PolicyQuotaController` struct that watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources
   - `NewPolicyQuotaController(client, informer, maxPerNamespace int)` constructor
   - `Run(ctx context.Context)` method implementing the controller loop
   - Per-namespace counting using a thread-safe map
   - `CheckQuota(namespace string) error` method that returns error if quota exceeded

2. **Create CRD type** `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_policy_quota.go`:
   - `CiliumPolicyQuota` struct with `Spec.MaxPoliciesPerNamespace` field
   - Follow existing Cilium CRD patterns (DeepCopy, runtime.Object)

3. **Create `pkg/policy/quota/controller_test.go`** with tests

4. **Follow Cilium patterns**:
   - Use `hive` dependency injection framework
   - Use `resource.Resource[T]` for watching K8s resources
   - Use `logfields` for structured logging

## Key Reference Files
- `pkg/policy/k8s/watcher.go` — CiliumNetworkPolicy watcher pattern
- `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_cnp.go` — CiliumNetworkPolicy CRD type
- `operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/` — controller using hive pattern
- `pkg/k8s/resource/resource.go` — resource watching framework

## Success Criteria
- PolicyQuotaController struct with Run method exists
- CheckQuota method performs namespace counting
- CiliumPolicyQuota CRD type exists
- Uses Cilium's hive/resource patterns
- Test file exists with test functions

I am thinking...: Now I have a thorough understanding of the codebase. Let me plan the three files:

## File 1: `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_policy_quota.go`

This defines the `CiliumNetworkPolicyQuota` CRD type. It should:
- Be a namespaced resource (per-namespace limits)
- Have a `Spec` with `MaxPolicies int32` (the limit)
- Have a `Status` with `CurrentCount int32` and `Enforced bool`
- Implement `runtime.Object` via `DeepCopyObject()`
- Follow the same pattern as `cnc_types.go` and `cegp_types.go`

## File 2: `pkg/policy/quota/controller.go`

This is the main controller. It should:
- Watch `CiliumNetworkPolicy` resources via `resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]`
- Watch `CiliumNetworkPolicyQuota` resources via `resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicyQuota]`
- Track per-namespace counts of CNPs
- Enforce limits defined in `CiliumNetworkPolicyQuota` objects
- Use `sync.RWMutex` for thread safety
- Use `cell.Lifecycle` for start/stop
- Use `logrus.FieldLogger` for logging
- Expose a `Run(ctx context.Context)` method

## File 3: `pkg/policy/quota/controller_test.go`

Tests for the controller using the `fakeResource` pattern from `helpers_test.go`.

Let me think about the controller design more carefully:

The controller needs to:
1. Watch CNP events (Upsert/Delete/Sync) to maintain a count per namespace
2. Watch CiliumNetworkPolicyQuota events to know the limits per namespace
3. When a CNP is upserted, check if the namespace has a quota and if the count exceeds it
4. If the count exceeds the quota, the controller should "enforce" it - but what does enforcement mean? Since we can't actually block the creation (that would require an admission webhook), the controller can:
   - Track violations
   - Log warnings
   - Update the quota status

### `types_policy_quota.go` — CRD type definition

Follows the exact same pattern as `cnc_types.go` / `cegp_types.go`:

- **`CiliumNetworkPolicyQuota`** — namespaced CRD (`scope="Namespaced"`). A quota object in namespace `foo` constrains CNPs in that same namespace. Embeds `metav1.TypeMeta` + `metav1.ObjectMeta` with `+deepequal-gen=false` markers (matching the rest of the v2 package).
- **`CiliumNetworkPolicyQuotaSpec`** — single field `MaxPolicies int32` with `+kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1`.
- **`CiliumNetworkPolicyQuotaStatus`** — `CurrentCount int32` (observed count) and `Enforced bool` (true when at or over quota).
- **`CiliumNetworkPolicyQuotaList`** — standard list wrapper required by the `runtime.Object` interface.
- Full kubebuilder marker set: `+genclient`, `+k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces`, `+kubebuilder:subresource:status`, `+kubebuilder:printcolumn` for all four fields.

DeepCopy methods were added to `zz_generated.deepcopy.go` in alphabetical order (between `CiliumNetworkPolicyList` and `CiliumNetworkPolicyNodeStatus`), matching the auto-generated style exactly.

Each event must be marked as handled\n    59\t\t// with a call to Done() which marks the key processed. No new events for this key\n    60\t\t// will be emitted before Done() is called.\n    61\t\t//\n    62\t\t// A missing Done() will lead to an eventual panic (via finalizer on Event[T]).\n    63\t\t// Panic on this situation is needed as otherwise no new events would be emitted\n    64\t\t// and thus this needs to be enforced.\n    65\t\t//\n    66\t\t// A stream of Upsert events are emitted first to replay the current state of the\n    67\t\t// store after which incremental upserts and deletes follow until the underlying\n    68\t\t// store is synchronized after which a Sync event is emitted and further incremental\n    69\t\t// updates:\n    70\t\t//\n    71\t\t//\t(start observing), Upsert, Upsert, Upsert, (done replaying store contents), Upsert, Upsert,\n    72\t\t//\t  (store synchronized with API server), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\n    73\t\t//\n    74\t\t// The emitting of the Sync event does not depend on whether or not Upsert events have\n    75\t\t// all been marked Done() without an error. The sync event solely signals that the underlying\n    76\t\t// store has synchronized and that Upsert events for objects in a synchronized store have been\n    77\t\t// sent to the observer.\n    78\t\t//\n    79\t\t// When Done() is called with non-nil error the error handler is invoked, which\n    80\t\t// can ignore, requeue the event (by key) or close the channel. The default error handler\n    81\t\t// will requeue.\n    82\t\t//\n    83\t\t// If an Upsert is retried and the object has been deleted, a Delete event will be emitted instead.\n    84\t\t// Conversely if a Delete event is retried and the object has been recreated with the same key,\n    85\t\t// an Upsert will be emitted instead.\n    86\t\t//\n    87\t\t// If an objects is created and immediately deleted, then a slow observer may not observe this at\n    88\t\t// all. In all cases a Delete event is only emitted if the observer has seen an Upsert. Whether or\n    89\t\t// not it had been successfully handled (via Done(nil)) does not affect this property.\n    90\t\tEvents(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T]\n    91\t\n    92\t\t// Store retrieves the read-only store for the resource. registers `OnStart`/`OnStop` hooks with `cell.Lifecycle`.\n- **`Run(ctx)`** \u2014 single `select` loop over both event channels; exits cleanly on context cancellation or closed channel.\n- **Warning logs** fire on every Upsert that pushes a namespace over its quota, and immediately when a quota is applied to a namespace already over the limit.\n- **`IsOverQuota(namespace) bool`** and **`NamespaceCount(namespace) int`** are the public query API.\n\n---\n\n#### 3. `pkg/policy/quota/controller_test.go` (new)\n13 deterministic unit tests using a `fakeResource[T]` channel-backed test double (same pattern as `pkg/egressgateway/helpers_test.go`).
